</th>
<td><span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Madrigals&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Madrigals</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Galliards&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Galliards</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Pavans&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Pavans</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Canzonas&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Canzonas</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Motets&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Motets</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:For_2_instruments&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">For 2 instruments</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Scores_with_open_instrumentation&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Scores with open instrumentation</a></span>; <th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>59 (actually 48) pieces
<dl><dd>1. Fuga [2 instruments]
</dd><dd>2. Fuga [2 instruments]

</dd><dd>4. Fuga [2 instruments]
</dd><dd>5. Fuga [2 instruments]

</dd><dd>7. Phantasia [2 instruments]
</dd><dd>8. Canzon [2 instruments]
</dd><dd>9. Madrigal "Die Brünnlein, die da fließen" [2 voices]
</dd><dd>10. Madrigal "Ich und du" [2 voices]
</dd><dd>11. Madrigal "O höchster Schatz" [2 voices]
</dd><dd>12. Madrigal "Ade, mein's Herzens Krönelein" [2 voices]
</dd><dd>13. Moteta "Duo abs te rogavi" [2 voices]
</dd><dd>14-23. Passametz, 10 variations [3 instruments]
</dd><dd>24. Fuga [3 instruments]
</dd><dd>25. Fuga [3 instruments]
</dd><dd>26. Phantasia [3 instruments]
</dd><dd>27. Madrigal "Der Liebste mein" [3 voices]
</dd><dd>28. Madrigal "Mein Herz nach Gottes Willen" [3 voices]
</dd><dd>29. Madrigal "Mit deiner Zucht" [3 voices]
</dd><dd>30. Moteta "Tria me exhilarant" [3 voices]
</dd><dd>31. Paduana [4 instruments]
</dd><dd>32. Paduana [4 instruments]
</dd><dd>33. Intrada [4 instruments]
</dd><dd>34. Intrada [4 instruments]
</dd><dd>35. Galliard [4 instruments]
</dd><dd>36. Tantz "Ein' Tochter bat die Mutter schon" [4 voices]
</dd><dd>37. Madrigal "Elend bringt Pein" [4 voices]
</dd><dd>38. Madrigal "Buhlschaft schad't neut" [4 voices]
</dd><dd>39. Galliard "Gar treu, aufrichtig, friedesam" [4 voices]
</dd><dd>40. Tantz "Einstmals ein Mägdlein frisch und jung" [4 voices]
</dd><dd>41. Paduana [4 instruments]
</dd><dd>42. Paduana [4 instruments]
</dd><dd>43. Intrada [4 instruments]
</dd><dd>44. Intrada [4 instruments]
</dd><dd>45. Galliard "Ach, ach groß Schmerz und Pein" [4 voices]
</dd><dd>46. Galliard [4 instruments]
</dd><dd>47. Madrigal "Vor Zeiten war die Tugend" [4 voices]
</dd><dd>48. Madrigal "Ich bin des reichen Bauren Sohn" [5 voices]
</dd><dd>49. Tantz [5 instruments]
</dd><dd>50. Tantz [5 instruments]
</dd><dd>51. Galliard "Ach Fräulein schon" [5 voices]
</dd><dd>52. Moteta "Vulnerasti cor meum" [5 voices]
</dd><dd>53. Cantzon [6 instruments]
</dd><dd>54-56. "Herzlich tut mich erfreuen" [6 voices]
</dd><dd>57. Madrigal "Schwer langweilig ist mir mein' Zeit" [6 voices]
</dd><dd>58. "Nachtwache" [7 voices]
</dd><dd>59. "Der ehlich Stand" [8 voices]
</dd></dl>
